<color\=#66ccff>特定召喚順序</color>=<color\=#66ccff>Specific Summon Order</color>
未同時擁有四種蔬菜騎士時，按照茄子騎士、馬鈴薯騎士、蘑菇騎士、蘆筍騎士的順序進行召喚；已同時擁有四種蔬菜騎士時，後續僅召喚馬鈴薯騎士。\n透過『蔬菜騎士·集合』首次召喚茄子騎士時，{{A}}自動變幻為『茄之紫』狀態。=When YUI doesn't have 4 kinds of Vegetable Knights, summon them in the order of Eggplant Knight, Potato Knight, Mushroom Knight, Asparagus Knight; When YUI has 4 kinds of Vegetable Knights, she will only summon Potato Knights.\nWhen YUI summon Eggplant Knight from [Vegetable Knights: Assemble] for the first time, change to [Eggplant Purple].
<color\=#66ccff>特定規則</color>=<color\=#66ccff>Specific Rules</color>
按下述優先順序，{{A}}在釋放HIGHLIGHT後會觸發處於不同狀態下的『蔬菜騎士·出擊』：\n1、HIGHLIGHT目標未處於『蘑菇孢子』狀態下，且自身擁有蘑菇騎士時，觸發處於『菇之粉』狀態的『蔬菜騎士·出擊』；\n2、自身未處於『塊莖之力』狀態下，且自身擁有馬鈴薯騎士時，觸發處於『薯之黃』狀態的『蔬菜騎士·出擊』；\n3、自身擁有茄子騎士時，觸發處於『茄之紫』狀態的『蔬菜騎士·出擊』；\n4、自身未擁有蔬菜騎士時，不觸發『蔬菜騎士·出擊』。=Based on the following priority, YUI will activate a different [Vegetable Knight: Strike] after using HIGHLIGHT:\n1. When the HIGHLIGHT target isn't inflicted with [Mushroom Spores] and YUI has Mushroom Knight, activate [Mushroom Pink] state [Vegetable Knight: Strike];\n2. When YUI doesn't have [Tuber Power] and has Potato Knight, activate [Potato Yellow] state [Vegetable Knight: Strike];\n3. When YUI has Eggplant Knight, activate [Eggplant Purple] state [Vegetable Knight: Strike];\n4. When YUI has no Vegetable Knights, do not activate [Vegetable Knight: Strike].

{{A}}的特殊戰鬥資源，用於釋放特殊技能『神諭轉換』。={{A}}'s special resource. Used to use the special skill [Oracle Shift].
<color\=#66ccff>『神諭轉換』</color>=<color\=#66ccff>[Oracle Shift]</color>
r:"^消耗(\d+)層『願望聆聽』，使當前回合所屬的友方角色（後稱『當前角色』）暫時退場並使『後備角色』登場並進行1次行動，『後備角色』行動後退場並重新替換為『當前角色』，『當前角色』繼續行動。\n『後備角色』登場時，會複製『當前角色』非自身添加的所有狀態（『後備角色』退場時會清除這些狀態）。『後備角色』初次登場時，會觸發所有"戰鬥開始時"的效果。『後備角色』退場時，所有狀態的持續時間不會減少。$"="Spend $1 [Wish Listener] stacks. The acting [Current Character] become inactive, the [Backup Character] become active and take 1 action. After this action, the [Backup Character] become inactive, and the [Current Character] become active to continue their turn. \nWhen the [Backup Character] is active, they copy all status effects from the [Current Character] except those they applied to themselves. These are cleared when the [Backup Character] become inactive. When the [Backup Character] first become active, activate all [Start of Battle] effects. When the [Backup Character] become inactive, do not affect the duration of effects with turn limits."
<color\=#66ccff>戰鬥輪次</color>=<color\=#66ccff>Combat Turn</color>
戰鬥中所有存活的友方角色都經過了1次非額外回合後，視為經過了1次戰鬥輪次。=After all alive allies take 1 non-Extra Action action, count as 1 combat turn.
<color\=#66ccff>後備角色</color>=<color\=#66ccff>Backup Character</color>
只在隊伍上陣{{A}}後，可以選擇一名未上陣的可使用角色作為{{A}}的『後備角色』；『後備角色』不視作編入隊伍，不計入戰鬥開局的屬性、職業、角色數量等；=Only after {{A}} is in the party, you can select 1 non-deployed character as {{A}}'s [Backup Character]; The [Backup Character] don't count as being in the party, and will not interact with start of battle attribute, role, character number, etc;
僅在隊伍上陣{{A}}後，可以選擇一名未上陣的可使用角色作為{{A}}的『後備角色』；『後備角色』不視作編入隊伍，不計入戰鬥開局的屬性、職業、角色數量等；=Only after {{A}} is in the party, you can select 1 non-deployed character as {{A}}'s [Backup Character]; The [Backup Character] don't count as being in the party, and will not interact with start of battle attribute, role, character number, etc;

<color\=#66ccff>面具強度</color>=<color\=#66ccff>Desire Level</color>
{{A}}&{{B}}的特色屬性，會影響釋放{{A}}&{{B}}技能部分效果的強度。=Influences the effects of certain skills based on stacks.
<color\=#66ccff>技能效果增幅</color>=<color\=#66ccff>Skill Effect Amp</color>
使{{A}}技能/戰鬥技巧中技能升級項的技能強度提升，該效果與其他加成效果獨立計算。對“受到角色屬性影響的效果”生效時，不會提升屬性的計入上限而直接對技能強度生效。=Increase the effects of skills/Thief Tactics that are increased when levelling up skills. This effect is calculated independently of other effects. For effects that influences the Phantom Thieves' stats, the stats increase cap will not be raised, but instead be applied directly as a skill effect.
<color\=#66ccff>相貌</color>=<color\=#66ccff>Facade</color>
{{A}}&{{B}}的特色資源，不同的相貌組合可以觸發技能『二元合一的面具』不同的效果。=The effects of [Two Masks as One] change depending on the combination of Facades gained.
<color\=#66ccff>進階屬性</color>=<color\=#66ccff>Effects Stats</color>
包含暴擊率、暴擊效果、穿透、傷害加成、弱點傷害等，可在角色屬性介面查看全部屬性。=Effect stats include Crit Rate, Crit DMG, Pierce, DMG Bonus, Weak DMG, and more.

雙子看守=Twin Wardens
r:"^獲得{{A}}&{{B}}後，WONDER的{{C}}技能和戰鬥技巧等級提升1級。（無論{{A}}&{{B}}是否在場）\n{{A}}&{{B}}擁有(\d+)組特殊的{{C}}，戰鬥開始前可以選擇兩組{{C}}作為自身的一技能和二技能進入戰鬥。\n{{A}}&{{B}}在攜帶不同的{{C}}組合時，在戰鬥中可以獲得對應的職業加成效果。\n頑皮與天真的面具\+奉獻與警示的面具：救援\n頑皮與天真的面具\+荒謬與悖理的面具：優越\n頑皮與天真的面具\+福果與禍因的面具：支配\n奉獻與警示的面具\+荒謬與悖理的面具：防護\n奉獻與警示的面具\+福果與禍因的面具：屈從\n荒謬與悖理的面具\+福果與禍因的面具：反抗\n{{A}}&{{B}}的技能效果受自身『<link\="s\|271"><u>面具強度</u></link>』影響，戰鬥開始時獲得(\d+)點『<link\="s\|271"><u>面具強度</u></link>』。$"="After obtaining Justine & Caroline, during battle, increase Wonder's skill and Thief Tactics levels by 1 (takes effect even when Justine & Caroline are not in battle).\nBefore entering battle, Justine & Caroline can select 2 of their $1 sets of Personas, and their Skill 1 and Skill 2 will change accordingly. During battle, Justine & Caroline will receive the following role effect based on the selected sets:\nMask of Mischief & Innocence + Mask of Service & Admonition: Medic\nMask of Mischief & Innocence + Mask of Absurdity & Nonsense: Strategist\nMask of Mischief & Innocence + Mask of Luck & Loss: Sweeper\nMask of Service & Admonition + Mask of Absurdity & Nonsense: Guardian\nMask of Service & Admonition + Mask of Luck & Loss: Saboteur\nMask of Absurdity & Nonsense + Mask of Luck & Loss: Assassin\nSkill effects are affected by [<link\="s|271"><u>Desire Level</u></link>].
